{"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01Dddfq5o8XV1MGKuFZtU4S6","type":"tool_result","content":".. raw:: html\n\n   <picture>\n      <source media=\"(prefers-color-scheme: light)\" srcset=\"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/cilium/cilium@main/Documentation/images/logo.png\" width=\"350\" alt=\"Cilium Logo\">\n      <img src=\"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/cilium/cilium@main/Documentation/images/logo-dark.png\" width=\"350\" alt=\"Cilium Logo\">\n   </picture>\n\n|cii| |go-report| |clomonitor| |artifacthub| |slack| |go-doc| |rtd| |apache| |bsd| |gpl| |fossa| |gateway-api| |codespaces|\n\nCilium is a networking, observability, and security solution with an eBPF-based\ndataplane. It provides a simple flat Layer 3 network with the ability to span\nmultiple clusters in either a native routing or overlay mode. It is L7-protocol\naware and can enforce network policies on L3-L7 using an identity based security\nmodel that is decoupled from network addressing.\n\nCilium implements distributed load balancing for traffic between pods and to\nexternal services, and is able to fully replace kube-proxy, using efficient\nhash tables in eBPF allowing for almost unlimited scale. It also supports\nadvanced functionality like integrated ingress and egress gateway, bandwidth\nmanagement and service mesh, and provides deep network and security visibility and monitoring.\n\nA new Linux kernel technology called eBPF_ is at the foundation of Cilium. It\nsupports dynamic insertion of eBPF bytecode into the Linux kernel at various\nintegration points such as: network IO, application sockets, and tracepoints to\nimplement security, networking and visibility logic. eBPF is highly efficient\nand flexible. To learn more about eBPF, visit `eBPF.io`_.\n\n.. image:: Documentation/images/cilium-overview.png\n   :alt: Overview of Cilium features for networking, observability, service mesh, and runtime security\n\nStable Releases\n===============\n\nThe Cilium community maintains minor stable releases for the last three minor\nCilium versions. The SBOM is generated in `SPDX`_ format. More information\non this is available on `Cilium SBOM`_.\n\n.. _`SPDX`: https://spdx.dev/\n.. _`Cilium SBOM`: https://docs.cilium.io/en/latest/configuration/sbom/\n\nDevelopment\n===========\n\nFor development and testing purpose, the Cilium community publishes snapshots,\nearly release candidates (RC) and CI container images build from the `main\nbranch <https://github.com/cilium/cilium/commits/main>`_. These images are\nnot for use in production.\n\nFor testing upgrades to new development releases please consult the latest\ndevelopment build of the `Cilium Upgrade Guide`_.\n\nListed below are branches for testing along with their snapshots or RC releases,\ncorresponding image pull tags and their release notes where applicable:\n\n+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+------------+----------------------------------------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+\n| `main <https://github.com/cilium/cilium/commits/main>`__                             | daily      | ``quay.io/cilium/cilium-ci:latest``          | N/A                                                                                       |\n+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+------------+----------------------------------------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+\n| `v1.16.0-rc.0 <https://github.com/cilium/cilium/commits/v1.16.0-rc.0>`__             | 2024-06-17 | ``quay.io/cilium/cilium:v1.16.0-rc.0``       | `Release Candidate Notes <https://github.com/cilium/cilium/releases/tag/v1.16.0-rc.0>`__  |\n+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+------------+----------------------------------------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+\n\nFunctionality Overview\n======================\n\n.. begin-functionality-overview\n\nProtect and secure APIs transparently\n-------------------------------------\n\nAbility to secure modern application protocols such as REST/HTTP, gRPC and\nKafka. Cilium\nprovides the ability to filter on individual application protocol requests such\nas:\n\n- Allow all HTTP requests with method ``GET`` and path ``/public/.*``. resources.\ntype PolicyQuotaController struct {\n\tlog logrus.FieldLogger\n\n\t// Resource for watching CiliumNetworkPolicy changes\n\tciliumNetworkPolicies resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy]\n\n\t// maxPerNamespace is the maximum number of policies allowed per namespace\n\tmaxPerNamespace int\n\n\t// mu protects policyCountByNamespace\n\tmu sync.RWMutex\n\n\t// policyCountByNamespace tracks the number of CiliumNetworkPolicy\n\t// resources in each namespace\n\tpolicyCountByNamespace map[string]int\n}\n\n// NewPolicyQuotaController creates a new PolicyQuotaController.\nfunc NewPolicyQuotaController(\n\tlog logrus.FieldLogger,\n\tciliumNetworkPolicies resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy],\n\tmaxPerNamespace int,\n) *PolicyQuotaController {\n\treturn &PolicyQuotaController{\n\t\tlog:                    log.WithField(logfields.LogSubsys, \"policy-quota\"),\n\t\tciliumNetworkPolicies:  ciliumNetworkPolicies,\n\t\tmaxPerNamespace:        maxPerNamespace,\n\t\tpolicyCountByNamespace: make(map[string]int),\n\t}\n}\n\n// Run starts the controller loop that watches for CiliumNetworkPolicy changes.\n// It blocks until the context is cancelled.\nfunc (pc *PolicyQuotaController) Run(ctx context.Context) error {\n\tpc.log.Info(\"Starting PolicyQuotaController\")\n\n\tevents := pc.ciliumNetworkPolicies.Events(ctx)\n\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n\t\t\tpc.log.Info(\"PolicyQuotaController stopped\")\n\t\t\treturn ctx.Err()\n\t\tcase event, ok := <-events:\n\t\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\t\tpc.log.Info(\"PolicyQuotaController events channel closed\")\n\t\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tvar err error\n\t\t\tswitch event.Kind {\n\t\t\tcase resource.Sync:\n\t\t\t\t// Synced indicates the resource has been fully synced\n\t\t\t\terr = nil\n\t\t\tcase resource.Upsert:\n\t\t\t\terr = pc.onPolicyUpsert(event.Object)\n\t\t\tcase resource.Delete:\n\t\t\t\terr = pc.onPolicyDelete(event.Object)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tevent.Done(err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// onPolicyUpsert handles an upserted CiliumNetworkPolicy.\nfunc (pc *PolicyQuotaController) onPolicyUpsert(policy *cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy) error {\n\tnamespace := policy.GetNamespace()\n\tname := policy.GetName()\n\n\tpc.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer pc.mu.Unlock()\n\n\t// If the policy already exists in our count, don't increment\n\t// (this is an update, not a new policy)\n\tif pc.policyCountByNamespace[namespace] > 0 {\n\t\t// Check if we need to count this as a new policy\n\t\t// by checking if it already existed\n\t\t// For now, we'll assume if it's being upserted, we pc.policyCountByNamespace[namespace],\n\t\t\"max_allowed\":          pc.maxPerNamespace,\n\t}).Debug(\"Policy count updated\")\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// onPolicyDelete handles a deleted CiliumNetworkPolicy.\nfunc (pc *PolicyQuotaController) onPolicyDelete(policy *cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy) error {\n\tnamespace := policy.GetNamespace()\n\tname := policy.GetName()\n\n\tpc.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer pc.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tif pc.policyCountByNamespace[namespace] > 0 {\n\t\tpc.policyCountByNamespace[namespace]--\n\t}\n\n\t// Clean up empty entries\n\tif pc.policyCountByNamespace[namespace] == 0 {\n\t\tdelete(pc.policyCountByNamespace, namespace)\n\t}\n\n\tpc.log.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.K8sNamespace: namespace,\n\t\tlogfields.K8sName:      name,\n\t\t\"policy_count\":         pc.policyCountByNamespace[namespace],\n\t}).Debug(\"Policy count decremented\")\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// CheckQuota checks if a namespace has exceeded its policy quota.\n// Returns nil if the quota has not been exceeded, or ErrQuotaExceeded if it has.\nfunc (pc *PolicyQuotaController) CheckQuota(namespace string) error {\n\tif pc.maxPerNamespace == 0 {\n\t\t// 0 means unlimited\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tpc.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer pc.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tcount := pc.policyCountByNamespace[namespace]\n\tif count >= pc.maxPerNamespace {\n\t\treturn event.Kind {\n\t\t\tcase resource.Sync:\n\t\t\t\t// Synced indicates the resource has been fully synced\n\t\t\t\terr = nil\n\t\t\tcase resource.Upsert:\n\t\t\t\terr = pc.onPolicyUpsert(event.Object)\n\t\t\tcase resource.Delete:\n\t\t\t\terr = pc.onPolicyDelete(event.Object)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tevent.Done(err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// onPolicyUpsert handles an upserted CiliumNetworkPolicy counted\")\n\t} else {\n\t\t// This is an update to an existing policy, no count change\n\t\tpc.log.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\t\tlogfields.K8sNamespace: namespace,\n\t\t\t\"name\":                 name,\n\t\t}).Debug(\"CiliumNetworkPolicy updated\")\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// onPolicyDelete handles a deleted CiliumNetworkPolicy.\nfunc (pc pc.policyCountByNamespace[namespace],\n\t}).Debug(\"Policy count decremented\")\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// CheckQuota checks if a namespace has exceeded its policy quota.\n// Returns nil if the quota has not been exceeded, or ErrQuotaExceeded if it has.\nfunc (pc *PolicyQuotaController) CheckQuota(namespace string) error {\n\tif pc.maxPerNamespace == 0 {\n\t\t// 0 means unlimited\n\t\treturn Controller Implementation\n**File:** `pkg/policy/quota/controller.go`\n\nMain controller implementation with:\n\n**`PolicyQuotaController` struct:**\n- `ciliumNetworkPolicies` - resource.Resource for watching CiliumNetworkPolicy\n- `maxPerNamespace` - maximum policies per namespace (0 = unlimited)\n- `policyCountByNamespace` - thread-safe map tracking policy counts\n- `policyKeys` - tracks which policies have been counted to distinguish updates from new policies\n- `mu` - sync.RWMutex for thread-safe access\n\n**Key methods:**\n\n- `NewPolicyQuotaController(log, ciliumNetworkPolicies, maxPerNamespace)` - Constructor\n  - Initializes the controller with logging and resource watching\n  - Sets up thread-safe maps for policy tracking\n\n- `Run(ctx context.Context) error` - Main controller loop\n  - Watches for resource events (Upsert, Delete, Sync)\n  - Processes events and calls appropriate handlers\n  - Blocks until context is cancelled\n\n- `CheckQuota(namespace string) error` - Quota checking method\n  - Returns nil if quota not exceeded\n  - Returns ErrQuotaExceeded with detailed message if exceeded\n  - Returns nil for unlimited quota (maxPerNamespace = 0)\n\n- `GetNamespaceCount(namespace string) int` - Query current policy count\n\n- `onPolicyUpsert(policy)` - Handles policy creation/updates\n  - Only increments count for new policies (tracked via policyKey)\n  - Updates not counted again (prevents double-counting)\n  - Logs at debug level\n\n- `onPolicyDelete(policy)` - Handles policy deletion\n  - Decrements count for tracked policies\n  - Cleans up empty namespace entries\n  - Warns if deletion event for unknown policy\n\n**Thread Safety:**\n- Uses `sync.RWMutex` for all access to shared state\n- Read locks for quota checking (fast path)\n- Write locks for updates\n\n### 3. Hive Integration\n**File:** `pkg/policy/quota/cell.go`\n\nProvides hive/cell integration for dependency injection:\n- Exports `Cell` module for Cilium's hive framework\n- `policyQuotaParams` struct for dependency injection\n- `newPolicyQuotaController` function to create controller instances\n- Configured with default unlimited quota (0)\n\n### 4. Package Documentation\n**File:** `pkg/policy/quota/doc.go`\n\nPackage-level documentation describing the quota enforcement purpose.\n\n### 5. Test Suite\n**File:** `pkg/policy/quota/controller_test.go`\n\nComprehensive test coverage including:\n\n**Test Functions:**\n1. `TestCheckQuota` - Quota checking with various scenarios\n   - Quota not exceeded\n   - Quota at limit (should fail)\n   - Quota exceeded (should fail)\n   - Unlimited quota (0)\n   - Unknown namespaces\n\n2. `TestGetNamespaceCount` - Namespace count queries\n   - Empty namespace\n   - Multiple namespaces\n   - Non-existent namespace\n\n3. `TestOnPolicyUpsert` - New policy and update handling\n   - New policy increments count\n   - Update to existing policy doesn't increment\n   - Multiple policies in namespace\n\n4. `TestOnPolicyDelete` - Policy deletion handling\n   - Deletion decrements count\n   - Cleanup of empty entries\n   - Deletion of unknown policies\n\n5. `TestControllerRunWithEvents` - Integration test\n   - Full event loop with mock resource\n   - Handles Upsert and Delete events\n   - Verifies count updates\n\n6. `TestNewPolicyQuotaController` - Constructor test\n   - Verifies proper initialization\n   - Checks all fields are set correctly\n\n**Mock Helpers:**\n- `mockEventChan` - Simulates event channel for testing\n- `mockResource` - Implements resource.Resource interface for testing\n\n## Design Decisions\n\n### Policy Tracking\n- Uses `namespace/name` key format to uniquely identify policies\n- Prevents double-counting of policy updates\n- Properly handles the replay of existing policies during initial sync\n\n### Error Handling\n- Custom `ErrQuotaExceeded` error for quota violation detection\n- Detailed error messages showing current count vs max allowed\n- Graceful handling of deletion events for unknown policies\n\n### Thread Safety\n- RWMutex allows concurrent quota checks (read locks)\n- Write locks only held during updates\n- Safe for concurrent access from multiple goroutines\n\n### Logging\n- Structured logging using Cilium's `logfields` package\n- Debug logs for normal operations\n- Warning logs for unexpected conditions\n\n## Cilium Patterns Used\n\n✅ **resource.Resource[T]** - For watching K8s resources\n✅ **logfields** - For structured logging\n✅ **hive/cell** - For dependency injection\n✅ **sync.RWMutex** - For thread-safe access\n✅ **kubebuilder markers** - For CRD generation\n✅ **SPDX licensing** - Following Cilium conventions\n\n## Usage Example\n\n```go\n// Create the controller\ncontroller := NewPolicyQuotaController(log, ciliumNetworkPolicies, 10)\n\n// Run the controller in a goroutine\ngo controller.Run(ctx)\n\n// Check quota before creating a new policy\nerr := controller.CheckQuota(\"default\")\nif err != nil {\n    // Quota exceeded, reject the policy\n}\n\n// Query current count\ncount := controller.GetNamespaceCount(\"default\")\n```\n\n## Testing\n\nAll tests pass the following scenarios:\n- Quota enforcement at limit and above\n- Proper tracking of new policies vs updates\n- Event handling for create, update, and delete\n- Thread-safe concurrent access\n- Cleanup of empty namespaces\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":0,"cache_creation_input_tokens":272,"cache_read_input_tokens":72609,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":272},"output_tokens":7,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"e97d971f-24d5-4c9d-a229-c0edaa4682f8","uuid":"8edb4980-e8ed-44ae-8758-c16d72689543"}
